  [user_task_description] # Requirements Document for 'JobBoard' Web Application  ## 1. Objective Develop a comprehensive web application named 'JobBoard' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to browse job postings, submit resumes, track applications, view company profiles, and manage job applications. No authentication required - all features are directly accessible. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.  ## 2. Language The required development language for the 'JobBoard' application is Python.  ## 3. Page Design  The 'JobBoard' web application will consist of the following nine pages:  ### 1. Dashboard Page - **Page Title**: Job Board Dashboard - **Overview**: The main hub displaying featured job postings, latest opportunities, and quick navigation to all functionalities. - **Elements**:   - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.   - **ID: featured-jobs** - Type: Div - Display of featured job recommendations.   - **ID: browse-jobs-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to job listings page.   - **ID: my-applications-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to applications tracking page.   - **ID: companies-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to companies directory page.  ### 2. Job Listings Page - **Page Title**: Job Listings - **Overview**: A page displaying all available job postings with search and filter capabilities. - **Elements**:   - **ID: listings-page** - Type: Div - Container for the listings page.   - **ID: search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search jobs by title, company, or location.   - **ID: category-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by job category (Technology, Finance, Healthcare, etc.).   - **ID: location-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by location (Remote, On-site, Hybrid).   - **ID: jobs-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying job cards with title, company, location, and salary range.   - **ID: view-job-button-{job_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view job details (each job card has this).  ### 3. Job Details Page - **Page Title**: Job Details - **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific job posting. - **Elements**:   - **ID: job-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the job details page.   - **ID: job-title** - Type: H1 - Display job title.   - **ID: company-name** - Type: Div - Display company name.   - **ID: job-description** - Type: Div - Display full job description and requirements.   - **ID: salary-range** - Type: Div - Display salary range.   - **ID: apply-now-button** - Type: Button - Button to apply for the job.  ### 4. Application Form Page - **Page Title**: Submit Application - **Overview**: A page for users to submit job applications with resume and cover letter. - **Elements**:   - **ID: application-form-page** - Type: Div - Container for the application form page.   - **ID: applicant-name** - Type: Input - Field to input applicant name.   - **ID: applicant-email** - Type: Input - Field to input applicant email.   - **ID: resume-upload** - Type: File Input - Field to upload resume file.   - **ID: cover-letter** - Type: Textarea - Field to enter cover letter text.   - **ID: submit-application-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit application.  ### 5. Application Tracking Page - **Page Title**: My Applications - **Overview**: A page displaying all submitted applications with status tracking. - **Elements**:   - **ID: tracking-page** - Type: Div - Container for the tracking page.   - **ID: applications-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying applications with job title, company, status, and date applied.   - **ID: status-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by status (All, Applied, Under Review, Interview, Rejected).   - **ID: view-application-button-{app_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view application details (each application has this).   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 6. Companies Directory Page - **Page Title**: Company Directory - **Overview**: A page displaying all registered companies with their profiles and available jobs. - **Elements**:   - **ID: companies-page** - Type: Div - Container for the companies page.   - **ID: companies-list** - Type: Div - List of company cards with company name, industry, and employee count.   - **ID: search-company-input** - Type: Input - Field to search companies by name or industry.   - **ID: view-company-button-{company_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view company profile (each company card has this).   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 7. Company Profile Page - **Page Title**: Company Profile - **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific company. - **Elements**:   - **ID: company-profile-page** - Type: Div - Container for the company profile page.   - **ID: company-info** - Type: Div - Display company name, industry, location, and description.   - **ID: company-jobs** - Type: Div - Display all open jobs from this company.   - **ID: jobs-list** - Type: Div - List of jobs with titles and status indicators.   - **ID: view-job-button-{job_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view job details from company profile.   - **ID: back-to-companies** - Type: Button - Button to go back to companies directory.  ### 8. Resume Management Page - **Page Title**: My Resumes - **Overview**: A page for users to upload and manage multiple resumes. - **Elements**:   - **ID: resume-page** - Type: Div - Container for the resume page.   - **ID: resumes-list** - Type: Div - List of uploaded resumes with upload date.   - **ID: upload-resume-button** - Type: Button - Button to upload a new resume.   - **ID: resume-file-input** - Type: File Input - Hidden file input for resume upload.   - **ID: delete-resume-button-{resume_id}** - Type: Button - Button to delete a resume (each resume has this).   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 9. Search Results Page - **Page Title**: Search Results - **Overview**: A page displaying search results for jobs and companies. - **Elements**:   - **ID: search-results-page** - Type: Div - Container for the search results page.   - **ID: search-query-display** - Type: Div - Display the search query entered.   - **ID: results-tabs** - Type: Div - Tabs to switch between job results and company results.   - **ID: job-results** - Type: Div - Display search results for jobs.   - **ID: company-results** - Type: Div - Display search results for companies.   - **ID: no-results-message** - Type: Div - Display when no results are found.  ## 4. Data Storage  The 'JobBoard' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:  ### 1. Jobs Data - **File Name**: `jobs.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   job_id|title|company_id|location|salary_min|salary_max|category|description|posted_date   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Senior Python Developer|1|Remote|80000|120000|Technology|Experienced Python developer for web applications|2025-01-15   2|Data Analyst|2|New York, NY|60000|85000|Finance|Analyze financial data and create reports|2025-01-16   3|Healthcare Administrator|3|Los Angeles, CA|50000|70000|Healthcare|Manage hospital operations and patient records|2025-01-14   ```  ### 2. Companies Data - **File Name**: `companies.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   company_id|company_name|industry|location|employee_count|description   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|TechCorp|Technology|San Francisco, CA|500|Leading software solutions provider   2|FinanceHub|Finance|New York, NY|300|Innovative financial services company   3|MediCare|Healthcare|Los Angeles, CA|200|Premier healthcare management organization   ```  ### 3. Categories Data - **File Name**: `categories.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   category_id|category_name|description   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Technology|Software, IT, and tech-related positions   2|Finance|Banking, accounting, and finance positions   3|Healthcare|Medical and healthcare industry positions   ```  ### 4. Applications Data - **File Name**: `applications.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   application_id|job_id|applicant_name|applicant_email|status|applied_date|resume_id   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|John Doe|john@email.com|Under Review|2025-01-17|1   2|2|Jane Smith|jane@email.com|Applied|2025-01-16|2   3|3|Robert Johnson|robert@email.com|Interview|2025-01-15|3   ```  ### 5. Resumes Data - **File Name**: `resumes.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   resume_id|applicant_name|applicant_email|filename|upload_date|summary   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|John Doe|john@email.com|john_resume.pdf|2025-01-17|Senior developer with 8 years experience   2|Jane Smith|jane@email.com|jane_resume.pdf|2025-01-16|Data analyst with financial background   3|Robert Johnson|robert@email.com|robert_resume.pdf|2025-01-15|Healthcare administrator with 5 years experience   ```  ### 6. Job Categories Mapping Data - **File Name**: `job_categories.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   mapping_id|job_id|category_id   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|1   2|2|2   3|3|3   ```

The app employs multiple templates rendered via Jinja2 and follows strict naming conventions and UI element IDs to facilitate developers.\n\n---\n\n## 1. Data Files (TXT Format)\nThe data files reside in a local 'data/' directory and use pipe-delimited formats for storage:\n\n- `jobs.txt`: Stores job postings with fields:\n  - `job_id|title|company_id|location|salary_min|salary_max|category|description|posted_date`\n\n- `companies.txt`: Stores companies with fields:\n  - `company_id|company_name|industry|location|employee_count|description`\n\n- `categories.txt`: Stores job categories with fields:\n  - `category_id|category_name|description`\n\n- `applications.txt`: Tracks user applications with fields:\n  - `application_id|job_id|applicant_name|applicant_email|status|applied_date|resume_id`\n\n- `resumes.txt`: Stores resumes uploaded by users:\n  - `resume_id|applicant_name|applicant_email|filename|upload_date|summary`\n\nAll files use straight pipe delimiter `|`. Dates format: `YYYY-MM-DD`.\n\n---\n\n## 2. Flask Routes and HTTP Methods\n\n### Frontend Routes\n\n- `/` [GET]\n  - Renders the **dashboard.html** page showing summary widgets and navigation buttons.\n  - Context variables:\n    - `jobs` (list of job dicts),\n    - `companies` (list of company dicts),\n    - `applications` (list of application dicts),\n    - `resumes` (list of resume dicts)\n\n- `/jobs` [GET]\n  - Renders **jobs-list.html** page.\n  - Context variables:\n    - `jobs` (filtered or all),\n    - `categories` (all job categories),\n    - `selected_category` (optional, int or None),\n    - `location_filter` (optional string)\n\n- `/job/<int:job_id>` [GET]\n  - Renders **job-details-page.html**.\n  - Context variables:\n    - `job` (single job dict),\n    - `company` (dict of associated company),\n    - `category` (category dict)\n\n- `/companies` [GET]\n  - Renders **companies-page.html**.\n  - Context variables:\n    - `companies` (list of companies)\n\n- `/company/<int:company_id>` [GET]\n  - Renders **company-profile-page.html**.\n  - Context variables:\n    - `company` (dict),\n    - `jobs` (list of job dict for company)\n\n- `/applications` [GET]\n  - Renders **applications-list.html**.\n  - Context variables:\n    - `applications` (all applications for user),\n    - `jobs` (dict keyed by job_id),\n    - `resumes` (dict keyed by resume_id)\n\n- `/application/<int:application_id>` [GET]\n  - Renders **application-details-page.html**.\n  - Context variables:\n    - `application` (dict),\n    - `job` (dict),\n    - `resume` (dict)\n\n- `/resumes` [GET]\n  - Renders **resumes-list.html**.\n  - Context variables:\n    - `resumes` (list of resumes)\n\n- `/upload_resume` [POST]\n  - Handles resume file upload form submission.\n\n- `/apply/<int:job_id>` [POST]\n  - Handles job application submission.\n\n- `/delete_resume/<int:resume_id>` [POST]\n  - Deletes resume specified.\n\n\n## 3. Navigation Elements and IDs\n\nThe app uses a consistent set of container IDs and button/element IDs in HTML templates to facilitate frontend manipulation and backend referencing.\n\n### Navigation Buttons\n\n- `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Returns to dashboard `/`\n- `browse-jobs-button` (Button): Navigate to `/jobs`\n- `companies-button` (Button): Navigate to `/companies`\n- `my-applications-button` (Button): Navigate to `/applications`\n- `upload-resume-button` (Button): Opens resume upload form\n\n### Search and Filters\n\n- `search-input` (Input text): Keyword search for jobs or companies\n- `category-filter` (Dropdown select): Filters jobs by category\n- `location-filter` (Input text): Filter jobs by location\n- `status-filter` (Dropdown select): Filter applications by status\n\n### Listings and Tables\n\n- `jobs-list` (Container Div): Holds grid/list of job cards\n- `job-results` (Div): Detailed job search results container\n- `companies-list` (Div): List companies\n- `applications-table` (Table): Lists all user applications\n- `resumes-list` (Table or Div): Lists resumes for user\n\n### Dynamic Buttons (Each render)\n\n- `view-job-button-{job_id}` (Button): View details of a specific job\n- `apply-now-button-{job_id}` (Button): Submit application for job\n- `view-company-button-{company_id}` (Button): View company profile\n- `view-application-button-{application_id}` (Button): View application details\n- `delete-resume-button-{resume_id}` (Button): Deletes the given resume\n\n\n## 4. Template Files and Context Variables\n\nAll templates located in the `templates/` directory use Jinja2 syntax. \n\n- `dashboard.html`\n  - Context: `jobs`, `companies`, `applications`, `resumes`\n  - Displays widgets summarizing data, with primary navigation buttons.\n\n- `jobs-list.html`\n  - Context: `jobs`, `categories`, `selected_category`, `location_filter`\n  - Displays search/filter inputs and job postings grid.\n\n- `job-details-page.html`\n  - Context: `job`, `company`, `category`\n  - Shows detailed job description with apply button.\n\n- `companies-page.html`\n  - Context: `companies`\n  - Displays company list with navigation buttons.\n\n- `company-profile-page.html`\n  - Context: `company`, `jobs`\n  - Show company details and current job postings.\n\n- `applications-list.html`\n  - Context: `applications`, `jobs`, `resumes`\n  - Shows user applications with statuses and links.\n\n- `application-details-page.html`\n  - Context: `application`, `job`, `resume`\n  - Detailed view of a single application including attached resume info.\n\n- `resumes-list.html`\n  - Context: `resumes`\n  - Lists user uploaded resumes with delete buttons.\n\n- `application-form-page.html`\n  - Context: `job`, `resumes`\n  - Form for users to apply for a job, selecting an existing resume or upload a new one.\n\n## 5. Detailed Example of a Route Implementation (Flask style)\n\n```python\n@app.route('/job/<int:job_id>', methods=['GET'])\ndef job_details(job_id):\n    job = get_job_by_id(job_id)\n    company = get_company_by_id(job['company_id'])\n    category = get_category_by_name(job['category'])\n    return render_template('job-details-page.html', job=job, company=company, category=category)\n```\n\nUse `url_for` in templates leveraging the above route definitions, e.g.: \n```\n<a id=\"view-job-button-{{ job.job_id }}\" href=\"{{ url_for('job_details', job_id=job.job_id) }}\">View Job</a>\n```\n\n## 6. Summary of IDs and their Types\n\n| ID Pattern | Element Type | Description |\n|-------------|--------------|-------------|\n| dashboard | Page Container Div | Main dashboard page container |\n| back-to-dashboard | Button | Navigation back to main dashboard |\n| browse-jobs-button | Button | Navigate to jobs listing |\n| companies-button | Button | Navigate to companies listing |\n| my-applications-button | Button | Navigate to applications listing |\n| jobs-list | Div | Container showing job-card elements |\n| view-job-button-{job_id} | Button | View the given job by job_id |\n| apply-now-button-{job_id} | Button | Apply for job_id |\n| applications-table | Table | Display applications user has submitted |\n| view-application-button-{app_id} | Button | View application detail |\n| delete-resume-button-{resume_id} | Button | Delete a resume by ID |\n\n---\n\nThis specification comprehensively covers backend routes, data schemas, page context variables, and UI element IDs for developers building or maintaining the JobBoard Flask application."})

  [design_spec.md] # JobBoard Application Design Specification  ## Overview This document details the Flask web application 'JobBoard' which enables users to browse jobs, view companies, track their applications, and manage resumes in a healthcare, technology, and finance job market environment. The app employs multiple templates rendered via Jinja2 and follows strict naming conventions and UI element IDs to facilitate developers.  ---  ## 1. Data Files (TXT Format) The data files reside in a local 'data/' directory and use pipe-delimited formats for storage:  - `jobs.txt`: Stores job postings with fields:   - `job_id|title|company_id|location|salary_min|salary_max|category|description|posted_date`  - `companies.txt`: Stores companies with fields:   - `company_id|company_name|industry|location|employee_count|description`  - `categories.txt`: Stores job categories with fields:   - `category_id|category_name|description`  - `applications.txt`: Tracks user applications with fields:   - `application_id|job_id|applicant_name|applicant_email|status|applied_date|resume_id`  - `resumes.txt`: Stores resumes uploaded by users:   - `resume_id|applicant_name|applicant_email|filename|upload_date|summary`  All files use straight pipe delimiter `|`. Dates format: `YYYY-MM-DD`.  ---  ## 2. Flask Routes and HTTP Methods  ### Frontend Routes  - `/` [GET]   - Renders the **dashboard.html** page showing summary widgets and navigation buttons.   - Context variables:     - `jobs` (list of job dicts),     - `companies` (list of company dicts),     - `applications` (list of application dicts),     - `resumes` (list of resume dicts)  - `/jobs` [GET]   - Renders **jobs-list.html** page.   - Context variables:     - `jobs` (filtered or all),     - `categories` (all job categories),     - `selected_category` (optional, int or None),     - `location_filter` (optional string)  - `/job/<int:job_id>` [GET]   - Renders **job-details-page.html**.   - Context variables:     - `job` (single job dict),     - `company` (dict of associated company),     - `category` (category dict)  - `/companies` [GET]   - Renders **companies-page.html**.   - Context variables:     - `companies` (list of companies)  - `/company/<int:company_id>` [GET]   - Renders **company-profile-page.html**.   - Context variables:     - `company` (dict),     - `jobs` (list of job dict for company)  - `/applications` [GET]   - Renders **applications-list.html**.   - Context variables:     - `applications` (all applications for user),     - `jobs` (dict keyed by job_id),     - `resumes` (dict keyed by resume_id)  - `/application/<int:application_id>` [GET]   - Renders **application-details-page.html**.   - Context variables:     - `application` (dict),     - `job` (dict),     - `resume` (dict)  - `/resumes` [GET]   - Renders **resumes-list.html**.   - Context variables:     - `resumes` (list of resumes)  - `/upload_resume` [POST]   - Handles resume file upload form submission.  - `/apply/<int:job_id>` [POST]   - Handles job application submission.  - `/delete_resume/<int:resume_id>` [POST]   - Deletes resume specified.   ## 3. Navigation Elements and IDs  The app uses a consistent set of container IDs and button/element IDs in HTML templates to facilitate frontend manipulation and backend referencing.  ### Navigation Buttons  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Returns to dashboard `/` - `browse-jobs-button` (Button): Navigate to `/jobs` - `companies-button` (Button): Navigate to `/companies` - `my-applications-button` (Button): Navigate to `/applications` - `upload-resume-button` (Button): Opens resume upload form  ### Search and Filters  - `search-input` (Input text): Keyword search for jobs or companies - `category-filter` (Dropdown select): Filters jobs by category - `location-filter` (Input text): Filter jobs by location - `status-filter` (Dropdown select): Filter applications by status  ### Listings and Tables  - `jobs-list` (Container Div): Holds grid/list of job cards - `job-results` (Div): Detailed job search results container - `companies-list` (Div): List companies - `applications-table` (Table): Lists all user applications - `resumes-list` (Table or Div): Lists resumes for user  ### Dynamic Buttons (Each render)  - `view-job-button-{job_id}` (Button): View details of a specific job - `apply-now-button-{job_id}` (Button): Submit application for job - `view-company-button-{company_id}` (Button): View company profile - `view-application-button-{application_id}` (Button): View application details - `delete-resume-button-{resume_id}` (Button): Deletes the given resume   ## 4. Template Files and Context Variables  All templates located in the `templates/` directory use Jinja2 syntax.   - `dashboard.html`   - Context: `jobs`, `companies`, `applications`, `resumes`   - Displays widgets summarizing data, with primary navigation buttons.  - `jobs-list.html`   - Context: `jobs`, `categories`, `selected_category`, `location_filter`   - Displays search/filter inputs and job postings grid.  - `job-details-page.html`   - Context: `job`, `company`, `category`   - Shows detailed job description with apply button.  - `companies-page.html`   - Context: `companies`   - Displays company list with navigation buttons.  - `company-profile-page.html`   - Context: `company`, `jobs`   - Show company details and current job postings.  - `applications-list.html`   - Context: `applications`, `jobs`, `resumes`   - Shows user applications with statuses and links.  - `application-details-page.html`   - Context: `application`, `job`, `resume`   - Detailed view of a single application including attached resume info.  - `resumes-list.html`   - Context: `resumes`   - Lists user uploaded resumes with delete buttons.  - `application-form-page.html`   - Context: `job`, `resumes`   - Form for users to apply for a job, selecting an existing resume or upload a new one.  ## 5. Detailed Example of a Route Implementation (Flask style)  ```python @app.route('/job/<int:job_id>', methods=['GET']) def job_details(job_id):     job = get_job_by_id(job_id)     company = get_company_by_id(job['company_id'])     category = get_category_by_name(job['category'])     return render_template('job-details-page.html', job=job, company=company, category=category) ```  Use `url_for` in templates leveraging the above route definitions, e.g.:  ``` <a id="view-job-button-{{ job.job_id }}" href="{{ url_for('job_details', job_id=job.job_id) }}">View Job</a> ```  ## 6. Summary of IDs and their Types  | ID Pattern | Element Type | Description | |-------------|--------------|-------------| | dashboard | Page Container Div | Main dashboard page container | | back-to-dashboard | Button | Navigation back to main dashboard | | browse-jobs-button | Button | Navigate to jobs listing | | companies-button | Button | Navigate to companies listing | | my-applications-button | Button | Navigate to applications listing | | jobs-list | Div | Container showing job-card elements | | view-job-button-{job_id} | Button | View the given job by job_id | | apply-now-button-{job_id} | Button | Apply for job_id | | applications-table | Table | Display applications user has submitted | | view-application-button-{app_id} | Button | View application detail | | delete-resume-button-{resume_id} | Button | Delete a resume by ID |  ---  This specification comprehensively covers backend routes, data schemas, page context variables, and UI element IDs for developers building or maintaining the JobBoard Flask application.
================================================================================

# Requirements Document for 'JobBoard' Web Application

## 1. Objective
Develop a comprehensive web application named 'JobBoard' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to browse job postings, submit resumes, track applications, view company profiles, and manage job applications. No authentication required - all features are directly accessible. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.

## 2. Language
The required development language for the 'JobBoard' application is Python.

## 3. Page Design

The 'JobBoard' web application will consist of the following nine pages:

### 1. Dashboard Page
- **Page Title**: Job Board Dashboard
- **Overview**: The main hub displaying featured job postings, latest opportunities, and quick navigation to all functionalities.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.
  - **ID: featured-jobs** - Type: Div - Display of featured job recommendations.
  - **ID: browse-jobs-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to job listings page.
  - **ID: my-applications-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to applications tracking page.
  - **ID: companies-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to companies directory page.

### 2. Job Listings Page
- **Page Title**: Job Listings
- **Overview**: A page displaying all available job postings with search and filter capabilities.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: listings-page** - Type: Div - Container for the listings page.
  - **ID: search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search jobs by title, company, or location.
  - **ID: category-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by job category (Technology, Finance, Healthcare, etc.).
  - **ID: location-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by location (Remote, On-site, Hybrid).
  - **ID: jobs-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying job cards with title, company, location, and salary range.
  - **ID: view-job-button-{job_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view job details (each job card has this).

### 3. Job Details Page
- **Page Title**: Job Details
- **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific job posting.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: job-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the job details page.
  - **ID: job-title** - Type: H1 - Display job title.
  - **ID: company-name** - Type: Div - Display company name.
  - **ID: job-description** - Type: Div - Display full job description and requirements.
  - **ID: salary-range** - Type: Div - Display salary range.
  - **ID: apply-now-button** - Type: Button - Button to apply for the job.

### 4. Application Form Page
- **Page Title**: Submit Application
- **Overview**: A page for users to submit job applications with resume and cover letter.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: application-form-page** - Type: Div - Container for the application form page.
  - **ID: applicant-name** - Type: Input - Field to input applicant name.
  - **ID: applicant-email** - Type: Input - Field to input applicant email.
  - **ID: resume-upload** - Type: File Input - Field to upload resume file.
  - **ID: cover-letter** - Type: Textarea - Field to enter cover letter text.
  - **ID: submit-application-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit application.

### 5. Application Tracking Page
- **Page Title**: My Applications
- **Overview**: A page displaying all submitted applications with status tracking.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: tracking-page** - Type: Div - Container for the tracking page.
  - **ID: applications-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying applications with job title, company, status, and date applied.
  - **ID: status-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by status (All, Applied, Under Review, Interview, Rejected).
  - **ID: view-application-button-{app_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view application details (each application has this).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 6. Companies Directory Page
- **Page Title**: Company Directory
- **Overview**: A page displaying all registered companies with their profiles and available jobs.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: companies-page** - Type: Div - Container for the companies page.
  - **ID: companies-list** - Type: Div - List of company cards with company name, industry, and employee count.
  - **ID: search-company-input** - Type: Input - Field to search companies by name or industry.
  - **ID: view-company-button-{company_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view company profile (each company card has this).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 7. Company Profile Page
- **Page Title**: Company Profile
- **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific company.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: company-profile-page** - Type: Div - Container for the company profile page.
  - **ID: company-info** - Type: Div - Display company name, industry, location, and description.
  - **ID: company-jobs** - Type: Div - Display all open jobs from this company.
  - **ID: jobs-list** - Type: Div - List of jobs with titles and status indicators.
  - **ID: view-job-button-{job_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view job details from company profile.
  - **ID: back-to-companies** - Type: Button - Button to go back to companies directory.

### 8. Resume Management Page
- **Page Title**: My Resumes
- **Overview**: A page for users to upload and manage multiple resumes.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: resume-page** - Type: Div - Container for the resume page.
  - **ID: resumes-list** - Type: Div - List of uploaded resumes with upload date.
  - **ID: upload-resume-button** - Type: Button - Button to upload a new resume.
  - **ID: resume-file-input** - Type: File Input - Hidden file input for resume upload.
  - **ID: delete-resume-button-{resume_id}** - Type: Button - Button to delete a resume (each resume has this).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 9. Search Results Page
- **Page Title**: Search Results
- **Overview**: A page displaying search results for jobs and companies.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: search-results-page** - Type: Div - Container for the search results page.
  - **ID: search-query-display** - Type: Div - Display the search query entered.
  - **ID: results-tabs** - Type: Div - Tabs to switch between job results and company results.
  - **ID: job-results** - Type: Div - Display search results for jobs.
  - **ID: company-results** - Type: Div - Display search results for companies.
  - **ID: no-results-message** - Type: Div - Display when no results are found.

## 4. Data Storage

The 'JobBoard' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:

### 1. Jobs Data
- **File Name**: `jobs.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  job_id|title|company_id|location|salary_min|salary_max|category|description|posted_date
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Senior Python Developer|1|Remote|80000|120000|Technology|Experienced Python developer for web applications|2025-01-15
  2|Data Analyst|2|New York, NY|60000|85000|Finance|Analyze financial data and create reports|2025-01-16
  3|Healthcare Administrator|3|Los Angeles, CA|50000|70000|Healthcare|Manage hospital operations and patient records|2025-01-14
  ```

### 2. Companies Data
- **File Name**: `companies.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  company_id|company_name|industry|location|employee_count|description
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|TechCorp|Technology|San Francisco, CA|500|Leading software solutions provider
  2|FinanceHub|Finance|New York, NY|300|Innovative financial services company
  3|MediCare|Healthcare|Los Angeles, CA|200|Premier healthcare management organization
  ```

### 3. Categories Data
- **File Name**: `categories.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  category_id|category_name|description
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Technology|Software, IT, and tech-related positions
  2|Finance|Banking, accounting, and finance positions
  3|Healthcare|Medical and healthcare industry positions
  ```

### 4. Applications Data
- **File Name**: `applications.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  application_id|job_id|applicant_name|applicant_email|status|applied_date|resume_id
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|John Doe|john@email.com|Under Review|2025-01-17|1
  2|2|Jane Smith|jane@email.com|Applied|2025-01-16|2
  3|3|Robert Johnson|robert@email.com|Interview|2025-01-15|3
  ```

### 5. Resumes Data
- **File Name**: `resumes.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  resume_id|applicant_name|applicant_email|filename|upload_date|summary
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|John Doe|john@email.com|john_resume.pdf|2025-01-17|Senior developer with 8 years experience
  2|Jane Smith|jane@email.com|jane_resume.pdf|2025-01-16|Data analyst with financial background
  3|Robert Johnson|robert@email.com|robert_resume.pdf|2025-01-15|Healthcare administrator with 5 years experience
  ```

### 6. Job Categories Mapping Data
- **File Name**: `job_categories.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  mapping_id|job_id|category_id
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|1
  2|2|2
  3|3|3
  ```


=== design_spec.md ===
# JobBoard Application Design Specification

## Overview
This document details the Flask web application 'JobBoard' which enables users to browse jobs, view companies, track their applications, and manage resumes in a healthcare, technology, and finance job market environment. The app employs multiple templates rendered via Jinja2 and follows strict naming conventions and UI element IDs to facilitate developers.

---

## 1. Data Files (TXT Format)
The data files reside in a local 'data/' directory and use pipe-delimited formats for storage:

- `jobs.txt`: Stores job postings with fields:
  - `job_id|title|company_id|location|salary_min|salary_max|category|description|posted_date`

- `companies.txt`: Stores companies with fields:
  - `company_id|company_name|industry|location|employee_count|description`

- `categories.txt`: Stores job categories with fields:
  - `category_id|category_name|description`

- `applications.txt`: Tracks user applications with fields:
  - `application_id|job_id|applicant_name|applicant_email|status|applied_date|resume_id`

- `resumes.txt`: Stores resumes uploaded by users:
  - `resume_id|applicant_name|applicant_email|filename|upload_date|summary`

All files use straight pipe delimiter `|`. Dates format: `YYYY-MM-DD`.

---

## 2. Flask Routes and HTTP Methods

### Frontend Routes

- `/` [GET]
  - Renders the **dashboard.html** page showing summary widgets and navigation buttons.
  - Context variables:
    - `jobs` (list of job dicts),
    - `companies` (list of company dicts),
    - `applications` (list of application dicts),
    - `resumes` (list of resume dicts)

- `/jobs` [GET]
  - Renders **jobs-list.html** page.
  - Context variables:
    - `jobs` (filtered or all),
    - `categories` (all job categories),
    - `selected_category` (optional, int or None),
    - `location_filter` (optional string)

- `/job/<int:job_id>` [GET]
  - Renders **job-details-page.html**.
  - Context variables:
    - `job` (single job dict),
    - `company` (dict of associated company),
    - `category` (category dict)

- `/companies` [GET]
  - Renders **companies-page.html**.
  - Context variables:
    - `companies` (list of companies)

- `/company/<int:company_id>` [GET]
  - Renders **company-profile-page.html**.
  - Context variables:
    - `company` (dict),
    - `jobs` (list of job dict for company)

- `/applications` [GET]
  - Renders **applications-list.html**.
  - Context variables:
    - `applications` (all applications for user),
    - `jobs` (dict keyed by job_id),
    - `resumes` (dict keyed by resume_id)

- `/application/<int:application_id>` [GET]
  - Renders **application-details-page.html**.
  - Context variables:
    - `application` (dict),
    - `job` (dict),
    - `resume` (dict)

- `/resumes` [GET]
  - Renders **resumes-list.html**.
  - Context variables:
    - `resumes` (list of resumes)

- `/upload_resume` [POST]
  - Handles resume file upload form submission.

- `/apply/<int:job_id>` [POST]
  - Handles job application submission.

- `/delete_resume/<int:resume_id>` [POST]
  - Deletes resume specified.


## 3. Navigation Elements and IDs

The app uses a consistent set of container IDs and button/element IDs in HTML templates to facilitate frontend manipulation and backend referencing.

### Navigation Buttons

- `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Returns to dashboard `/`
- `browse-jobs-button` (Button): Navigate to `/jobs`
- `companies-button` (Button): Navigate to `/companies`
- `my-applications-button` (Button): Navigate to `/applications`
- `upload-resume-button` (Button): Opens resume upload form

### Search and Filters

- `search-input` (Input text): Keyword search for jobs or companies
- `category-filter` (Dropdown select): Filters jobs by category
- `location-filter` (Input text): Filter jobs by location
- `status-filter` (Dropdown select): Filter applications by status

### Listings and Tables

- `jobs-list` (Container Div): Holds grid/list of job cards
- `job-results` (Div): Detailed job search results container
- `companies-list` (Div): List companies
- `applications-table` (Table): Lists all user applications
- `resumes-list` (Table or Div): Lists resumes for user

### Dynamic Buttons (Each render)

- `view-job-button-{job_id}` (Button): View details of a specific job
- `apply-now-button-{job_id}` (Button): Submit application for job
- `view-company-button-{company_id}` (Button): View company profile
- `view-application-button-{application_id}` (Button): View application details
- `delete-resume-button-{resume_id}` (Button): Deletes the given resume


## 4. Template Files and Context Variables

All templates located in the `templates/` directory use Jinja2 syntax. 

- `dashboard.html`
  - Context: `jobs`, `companies`, `applications`, `resumes`
  - Displays widgets summarizing data, with primary navigation buttons.

- `jobs-list.html`
  - Context: `jobs`, `categories`, `selected_category`, `location_filter`
  - Displays search/filter inputs and job postings grid.

- `job-details-page.html`
  - Context: `job`, `company`, `category`
  - Shows detailed job description with apply button.

- `companies-page.html`
  - Context: `companies`
  - Displays company list with navigation buttons.

- `company-profile-page.html`
  - Context: `company`, `jobs`
  - Show company details and current job postings.

- `applications-list.html`
  - Context: `applications`, `jobs`, `resumes`
  - Shows user applications with statuses and links.

- `application-details-page.html`
  - Context: `application`, `job`, `resume`
  - Detailed view of a single application including attached resume info.

- `resumes-list.html`
  - Context: `resumes`
  - Lists user uploaded resumes with delete buttons.

- `application-form-page.html`
  - Context: `job`, `resumes`
  - Form for users to apply for a job, selecting an existing resume or upload a new one.

## 5. Detailed Example of a Route Implementation (Flask style)

```python
@app.route('/job/<int:job_id>', methods=['GET'])
def job_details(job_id):
    job = get_job_by_id(job_id)
    company = get_company_by_id(job['company_id'])
    category = get_category_by_name(job['category'])
    return render_template('job-details-page.html', job=job, company=company, category=category)
```

Use `url_for` in templates leveraging the above route definitions, e.g.: 
```
<a id="view-job-button-{{ job.job_id }}" href="{{ url_for('job_details', job_id=job.job_id) }}">View Job</a>
```

## 6. Summary of IDs and their Types

| ID Pattern | Element Type | Description |
|-------------|--------------|-------------|
| dashboard | Page Container Div | Main dashboard page container |
| back-to-dashboard | Button | Navigation back to main dashboard |
| browse-jobs-button | Button | Navigate to jobs listing |
| companies-button | Button | Navigate to companies listing |
| my-applications-button | Button | Navigate to applications listing |
| jobs-list | Div | Container showing job-card elements |
| view-job-button-{job_id} | Button | View the given job by job_id |
| apply-now-button-{job_id} | Button | Apply for job_id |
| applications-table | Table | Display applications user has submitted |
| view-application-button-{app_id} | Button | View application detail |
| delete-resume-button-{resume_id} | Button | Delete a resume by ID |

---

This specification comprehensively covers backend routes, data schemas, page context variables, and UI element IDs for developers building or maintaining the JobBoard Flask application.

Application Form Page - **Page Title**: Submit Application - **Overview**: A page for users to submit job applications with resume and cover letter. - **Elements**:   - **ID: application-form-page** - Type: Div - Container for the application form page.   - **ID: applicant-name** - Type: Input - Field to input applicant name.   - **ID: applicant-email** - Type: Input - Field to input applicant email.   - **ID: resume-upload** - Type: File Input - Field to upload resume file.   - **ID: cover-letter** - Type: Textarea - Field to enter cover letter text.   - **ID: submit-application-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit application.  ### 5. Application Tracking Page - **Page Title**: My Applications - **Overview**: A page displaying all submitted applications with status tracking. - **Elements**:   - **ID: tracking-page** - Type: Div - Container for the tracking page.   - **ID: applications-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying applications with job title, company, status, and date applied.   - **ID: status-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by status (All, Applied, Under Review, Interview, Rejected).   - **ID: view-application-button-{app_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view application details (each application has this).   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 6. Companies Directory Page - **Page Title**: Company Directory - **Overview**: A page displaying all registered companies with their profiles and available jobs. - **Elements**:   - **ID: companies-page** - Type: Div - Container for the companies page.   - **ID: companies-list** - Type: Div - List of company cards with company name, industry, and employee count.   - **ID: search-company-input** - Type: Input - Field to search companies by name or industry.   - **ID: view-company-button-{company_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view company profile (each company card has this).   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 7. Company Profile Page - **Page Title**: Company Profile - **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific company. - **Elements**:   - **ID: company-profile-page** - Type: Div - Container for the company profile page.   - **ID: company-info** - Type: Div - Display company name, industry, location, and description.   - **ID: company-jobs** - Type: Div - Display all open jobs from this company.   - **ID: jobs-list** - Type: Div - List of jobs with titles and status indicators.   - **ID: view-job-button-{job_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view job details from company profile.   - **ID: back-to-companies** - Type: Button - Button to go back to companies directory.  ### 8. Resume Management Page - **Page Title**: My Resumes - **Overview**: A page for users to upload and manage multiple resumes. - **Elements**:   - **ID: resume-page** - Type: Div - Container for the resume page.   - **ID: resumes-list** - Type: Div - List of uploaded resumes with upload date.   - **ID: upload-resume-button** - Type: Button - Button to upload a new resume.   - **ID: resume-file-input** - Type: File Input - Hidden file input for resume upload.   - **ID: delete-resume-button-{resume_id}** - Type: Button - Button to delete a resume (each resume has this).   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 9. Search Results Page - **Page Title**: Search Results - **Overview**: A page displaying search results for jobs and companies. - **Elements**:   - **ID: search-results-page** - Type: Div - Container for the search results page.   - **ID: search-query-display** - Type: Div - Display the search query entered.   - **ID: results-tabs** - Type: Div - Tabs to switch between job results and company results.   - **ID: job-results** - Type: Div - Display search results for jobs.   - **ID: company-results** - Type: Div - Display search results for companies.   - **ID: no-results-message** - Type: Div - Display when no results are found.  ## 4. Data Storage  The 'JobBoard' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:  ### 1. Jobs Data - **File Name**: `jobs.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   job_id|title|company_id|location|salary_min|salary_max|category|description|posted_date   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Senior Python Developer|1|Remote|80000|120000|Technology|Experienced Python developer for web applications|2025-01-15   2|Data Analyst|2|New York, NY|60000|85000|Finance|Analyze financial data and create reports|2025-01-16   3|Healthcare Administrator|3|Los Angeles, CA|50000|70000|Healthcare|Manage hospital operations and patient records|2025-01-14   ```  ### 2. Companies Data - **File Name**: `companies.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   company_id|company_name|industry|location|employee_count|description   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|TechCorp|Technology|San Francisco, CA|500|Leading software solutions provider   2|FinanceHub|Finance|New York, NY|300|Innovative financial services company   3|MediCare|Healthcare|Los Angeles, CA|200|Premier healthcare management organization   ```  ### 3. Categories Data - **File Name**: `categories.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   category_id|category_name|description   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Technology|Software, IT, and tech-related positions   2|Finance|Banking, accounting, and finance positions   3|Healthcare|Medical and healthcare industry positions   ```  ### 4. Applications Data - **File Name**: `applications.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   application_id|job_id|applicant_name|applicant_email|status|applied_date|resume_id   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|John Doe|john@email.com|Under Review|2025-01-17|1   2|2|Jane Smith|jane@email.com|Applied|2025-01-16|2   3|3|Robert Johnson|robert@email.com|Interview|2025-01-15|3   ```  ### 5. Resumes Data - **File Name**: `resumes.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   resume_id|applicant_name|applicant_email|filename|upload_date|summary   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|John Doe|john@email.com|john_resume.pdf|2025-01-17|Senior developer with 8 years experience   2|Jane Smith|jane@email.com|jane_resume.pdf|2025-01-16|Data analyst with financial background   3|Robert Johnson|robert@email.com|robert_resume.pdf|2025-01-15|Healthcare administrator with 5 years experience   ```  ### 6. Job Categories Mapping Data - **File Name**: `job_categories.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   mapping_id|job_id|category_id   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|1   2|2|2   3|3|3   ```
  [design_spec.md] # JobBoard Application Design Specification  ## Overview This document details the Flask web application 'JobBoard' which enables users to browse jobs, view companies, track their applications, and manage resumes in a healthcare, technology, and finance job market environment. The app employs multiple templates rendered via Jinja2 and follows strict naming conventions and UI element IDs to facilitate developers.  ---  ## 1. Data Files (TXT Format) The data files reside in a local 'data/' directory and use pipe-delimited formats for storage:  - `jobs.txt`: Stores job postings with fields:   - `job_id|title|company_id|location|salary_min|salary_max|category|description|posted_date`  - `companies.txt`: Stores companies with fields:   - `company_id|company_name|industry|location|employee_count|description`  - `categories.txt`: Stores job categories with fields:   - `category_id|category_name|description`  - `applications.txt`: Tracks user applications with fields:   - `application_id|job_id|applicant_name|applicant_email|status|applied_date|resume_id`  - `resumes.txt`: Stores resumes uploaded by users:   - `resume_id|applicant_name|applicant_email|filename|upload_date|summary`  All files use straight pipe delimiter `|`. Dates format: `YYYY-MM-DD`.  ---  ## 2. Flask Routes and HTTP Methods  ### Frontend Routes  - `/` [GET]   - Renders the **dashboard.html** page showing summary widgets and navigation buttons.   - Context variables:     - `jobs` (list of job dicts),     - `companies` (list of company dicts),     - `applications` (list of application dicts),     - `resumes` (list of resume dicts)  - `/jobs` [GET]   - Renders **jobs-list.html** page.   - Context variables:     - `jobs` (filtered or all),     - `categories` (all job categories),     - `selected_category` (optional, int or None),     - `location_filter` (optional string)  - `/job/<int:job_id>` [GET]   - Renders **job-details-page.html**.   - Context variables:     - `job` (single job dict),     - `company` (dict of associated company),     - `category` (category dict)  - `/companies` [GET]   - Renders **companies-page.html**.   - Context variables:     - `companies` (list of companies)  - `/company/<int:company_id>` [GET]   - Renders **company-profile-page.html**.   - Context variables:     - `company` (dict),     - `jobs` (list of job dict for company)  - `/applications` [GET]   - Renders **applications-list.html**.   - Context variables:     - `applications` (all applications for user),     - `jobs` (dict keyed by job_id),     - `resumes` (dict keyed by resume_id)  - `/application/<int:application_id>` [GET]   - Renders **application-details-page.html**.   - Context variables:     - `application` (dict),     - `job` (dict),     - `resume` (dict)  - `/resumes` [GET]   - Renders **resumes-list.html**.   - Context variables:     - `resumes` (list of resumes)  - `/upload_resume` [POST]   - Handles resume file upload form submission.  - `/apply/<int:job_id>` [POST]   - Handles job application submission.  - `/delete_resume/<int:resume_id>` [POST]   - Deletes resume specified.   ## 3. Navigation Elements and IDs  The app uses a consistent set of container IDs and button/element IDs in HTML templates to facilitate frontend manipulation and backend referencing.  ### Navigation Buttons  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Returns to dashboard `/` - `browse-jobs-button` (Button): Navigate to `/jobs` - `companies-button` (Button): Navigate to `/companies` - `my-applications-button` (Button): Navigate to `/applications` - `upload-resume-button` (Button): Opens resume upload form  ### Search and Filters  - `search-input` (Input text): Keyword search for jobs or companies - `category-filter` (Dropdown select): Filters jobs by category - `location-filter` (Input text): Filter jobs by location - `status-filter` (Dropdown select): Filter applications by status  ### Listings and Tables  - `jobs-list` (Container Div): Holds grid/list of job cards - `job-results` (Div): Detailed job search results container - `companies-list` (Div): List companies - `applications-table` (Table): Lists all user applications - `resumes-list` (Table or Div): Lists resumes for user  ### Dynamic Buttons (Each render)  - `view-job-button-{job_id}` (Button): View details of a specific job - `apply-now-button-{job_id}` (Button): Submit application for job - `view-company-button-{company_id}` (Button): View company profile - `view-application-button-{application_id}` (Button): View application details - `delete-resume-button-{resume_id}` (Button): Deletes the given resume   ## 4. Template Files and Context Variables  All templates located in the `templates/` directory use Jinja2 syntax.   - `dashboard.html`   - Context: `jobs`, `companies`, `applications`, `resumes`   - Displays widgets summarizing data, with primary navigation buttons.  - `jobs-list.html`   - Context: `jobs`, `categories`, `selected_category`, `location_filter`   - Displays search/filter inputs and job postings grid.  - `job-details-page.html`   - Context: `job`, `company`, `category`   - Shows detailed job description with apply button.  - `companies-page.html`   - Context: `companies`   - Displays company list with navigation buttons.  - `company-profile-page.html`   - Context: `company`, `jobs`   - Show company details and current job postings.  - `applications-list.html`   - Context: `applications`, `jobs`, `resumes`   - Shows user applications with statuses and links.  - `application-details-page.html`   - Context: `application`, `job`, `resume`   - Detailed view of a single application including attached resume info.  - `resumes-list.html`   - Context: `resumes`   - Lists user uploaded resumes with delete buttons.  - `application-form-page.html`   - Context: `job`, `resumes`   - Form for users to apply for a job, selecting an existing resume or upload a new one.  ## 5. Detailed Example of a Route Implementation (Flask style)  ```python @app.route('/job/<int:job_id>', methods=['GET']) def job_details(job_id):     job = get_job_by_id(job_id)     company = get_company_by_id(job['company_id'])     category = get_category_by_name(job['category'])     return render_template('job-details-page.html', job=job, company=company, category=category) ```  Use `url_for` in templates leveraging the above route definitions, e.g.:  ``` <a id="view-job-button-{{ job.job_id }}" href="{{ url_for('job_details', job_id=job.job_id) }}">View Job</a> ```  ## 6. Summary of IDs and their Types  | ID Pattern | Element Type | Description | |-------------|--------------|-------------| | dashboard | Page Container Div | Main dashboard page container | | back-to-dashboard | Button | Navigation back to main dashboard | | browse-jobs-button | Button | Navigate to jobs listing | | companies-button | Button | Navigate to companies listing | | my-applications-button | Button | Navigate to applications listing | | jobs-list | Div | Container showing job-card elements | | view-job-button-{job_id} | Button | View the given job by job_id | | apply-now-button-{job_id} | Button | Apply for job_id | | applications-table | Table | Display applications user has submitted | | view-application-button-{app_id} | Button | View application detail | | delete-resume-button-{resume_id} | Button | Delete a resume by ID |  ---  This specification comprehensively covers backend routes, data schemas, page context variables, and UI element IDs for developers building or maintaining the JobBoard Flask application.
================================================================================

# Requirements Document for 'JobBoard' Web Application

## 1. Objective
Develop a comprehensive web application named 'JobBoard' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to browse job postings, submit resumes, track applications, view company profiles, and manage job applications. No authentication required - all features are directly accessible. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.

## 2. Language
The required development language for the 'JobBoard' application is Python.

## 3. Page Design

The 'JobBoard' web application will consist of the following nine pages:

### 1. Dashboard Page
- **Page Title**: Job Board Dashboard
- **Overview**: The main hub displaying featured job postings, latest opportunities, and quick navigation to all functionalities.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.
  - **ID: featured-jobs** - Type: Div - Display of featured job recommendations.
  - **ID: browse-jobs-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to job listings page.
  - **ID: my-applications-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to applications tracking page.
  - **ID: companies-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to companies directory page.

### 2. Job Listings Page
- **Page Title**: Job Listings
- **Overview**: A page displaying all available job postings with search and filter capabilities.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: listings-page** - Type: Div - Container for the listings page.
  - **ID: search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search jobs by title, company, or location.
  - **ID: category-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by job category (Technology, Finance, Healthcare, etc.).
  - **ID: location-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by location (Remote, On-site, Hybrid).
  - **ID: jobs-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying job cards with title, company, location, and salary range.
  - **ID: view-job-button-{job_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view job details (each job card has this).

### 3. Job Details Page
- **Page Title**: Job Details
- **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific job posting.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: job-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the job details page.
  - **ID: job-title** - Type: H1 - Display job title.
  - **ID: company-name** - Type: Div - Display company name.
  - **ID: job-description** - Type: Div - Display full job description and requirements.
  - **ID: salary-range** - Type: Div - Display salary range.
  - **ID: apply-now-button** - Type: Button - Button to apply for the job.

### 4. Application Form Page
- **Page Title**: Submit Application
- **Overview**: A page for users to submit job applications with resume and cover letter.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: application-form-page** - Type: Div - Container for the application form page.
  - **ID: applicant-name** - Type: Input - Field to input applicant name.
  - **ID: applicant-email** - Type: Input - Field to input applicant email.
  - **ID: resume-upload** - Type: File Input - Field to upload resume file.
  - **ID: cover-letter** - Type: Textarea - Field to enter cover letter text.
  - **ID: submit-application-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit application.

### 5. Application Tracking Page
- **Page Title**: My Applications
- **Overview**: A page displaying all submitted applications with status tracking.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: tracking-page** - Type: Div - Container for the tracking page.
  - **ID: applications-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying applications with job title, company, status, and date applied.
  - **ID: status-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by status (All, Applied, Under Review, Interview, Rejected).
  - **ID: view-application-button-{app_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view application details (each application has this).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 6. Companies Directory Page
- **Page Title**: Company Directory
- **Overview**: A page displaying all registered companies with their profiles and available jobs.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: companies-page** - Type: Div - Container for the companies page.
  - **ID: companies-list** - Type: Div - List of company cards with company name, industry, and employee count.
  - **ID: search-company-input** - Type: Input - Field to search companies by name or industry.
  - **ID: view-company-button-{company_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view company profile (each company card has this).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 7. Company Profile Page
- **Page Title**: Company Profile
- **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific company.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: company-profile-page** - Type: Div - Container for the company profile page.
  - **ID: company-info** - Type: Div - Display company name, industry, location, and description.
  - **ID: company-jobs** - Type: Div - Display all open jobs from this company.
  - **ID: jobs-list** - Type: Div - List of jobs with titles and status indicators.
  - **ID: view-job-button-{job_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view job details from company profile.
  - **ID: back-to-companies** - Type: Button - Button to go back to companies directory.

### 8. Resume Management Page
- **Page Title**: My Resumes
- **Overview**: A page for users to upload and manage multiple resumes.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: resume-page** - Type: Div - Container for the resume page.
  - **ID: resumes-list** - Type: Div - List of uploaded resumes with upload date.
  - **ID: upload-resume-button** - Type: Button - Button to upload a new resume.
  - **ID: resume-file-input** - Type: File Input - Hidden file input for resume upload.
  - **ID: delete-resume-button-{resume_id}** - Type: Button - Button to delete a resume (each resume has this).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 9. Search Results Page
- **Page Title**: Search Results
- **Overview**: A page displaying search results for jobs and companies.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: search-results-page** - Type: Div - Container for the search results page.
  - **ID: search-query-display** - Type: Div - Display the search query entered.
  - **ID: results-tabs** - Type: Div - Tabs to switch between job results and company results.
  - **ID: job-results** - Type: Div - Display search results for jobs.
  - **ID: company-results** - Type: Div - Display search results for companies.
  - **ID: no-results-message** - Type: Div - Display when no results are found.

## 4. Data Storage

The 'JobBoard' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:

### 1. Jobs Data
- **File Name**: `jobs.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  job_id|title|company_id|location|salary_min|salary_max|category|description|posted_date
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Senior Python Developer|1|Remote|80000|120000|Technology|Experienced Python developer for web applications|2025-01-15
  2|Data Analyst|2|New York, NY|60000|85000|Finance|Analyze financial data and create reports|2025-01-16
  3|Healthcare Administrator|3|Los Angeles, CA|50000|70000|Healthcare|Manage hospital operations and patient records|2025-01-14
  ```

### 2. Companies Data
- **File Name**: `companies.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  company_id|company_name|industry|location|employee_count|description
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|TechCorp|Technology|San Francisco, CA|500|Leading software solutions provider
  2|FinanceHub|Finance|New York, NY|300|Innovative financial services company
  3|MediCare|Healthcare|Los Angeles, CA|200|Premier healthcare management organization
  ```

### 3. Categories Data
- **File Name**: `categories.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  category_id|category_name|description
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Technology|Software, IT, and tech-related positions
  2|Finance|Banking, accounting, and finance positions
  3|Healthcare|Medical and healthcare industry positions
  ```

### 4. Applications Data
- **File Name**: `applications.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  application_id|job_id|applicant_name|applicant_email|status|applied_date|resume_id
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|John Doe|john@email.com|Under Review|2025-01-17|1
  2|2|Jane Smith|jane@email.com|Applied|2025-01-16|2
  3|3|Robert Johnson|robert@email.com|Interview|2025-01-15|3
  ```

### 5. Resumes Data
- **File Name**: `resumes.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  resume_id|applicant_name|applicant_email|filename|upload_date|summary
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|John Doe|john@email.com|john_resume.pdf|2025-01-17|Senior developer with 8 years experience
  2|Jane Smith|jane@email.com|jane_resume.pdf|2025-01-16|Data analyst with financial background
  3|Robert Johnson|robert@email.com|robert_resume.pdf|2025-01-15|Healthcare administrator with 5 years experience
  ```

### 6. Job Categories Mapping Data
- **File Name**: `job_categories.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  mapping_id|job_id|category_id
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|1
  2|2|2
  3|3|3
  ```


=== design_spec.md ===
# JobBoard Application Design Specification

## Overview
This document details the Flask web application 'JobBoard' which enables users to browse jobs, view companies, track their applications, and manage resumes in a healthcare, technology, and finance job market environment. The app employs multiple templates rendered via Jinja2 and follows strict naming conventions and UI element IDs to facilitate developers.

---

## 1. Data Files (TXT Format)
The data files reside in a local 'data/' directory and use pipe-delimited formats for storage:

- `jobs.txt`: Stores job postings with fields:
  - `job_id|title|company_id|location|salary_min|salary_max|category|description|posted_date`

- `companies.txt`: Stores companies with fields:
  - `company_id|company_name|industry|location|employee_count|description`

- `categories.txt`: Stores job categories with fields:
  - `category_id|category_name|description`

- `applications.txt`: Tracks user applications with fields:
  - `application_id|job_id|applicant_name|applicant_email|status|applied_date|resume_id`

- `resumes.txt`: Stores resumes uploaded by users:
  - `resume_id|applicant_name|applicant_email|filename|upload_date|summary`

All files use straight pipe delimiter `|`. Dates format: `YYYY-MM-DD`.

---

## 2. Flask Routes and HTTP Methods

### Frontend Routes

- `/` [GET]
  - Renders the **dashboard.html** page showing summary widgets and navigation buttons.
  - Context variables:
    - `jobs` (list of job dicts),
    - `companies` (list of company dicts),
    - `applications` (list of application dicts),
    - `resumes` (list of resume dicts)

- `/jobs` [GET]
  - Renders **jobs-list.html** page.
  - Context variables:
    - `jobs` (filtered or all),
    - `categories` (all job categories),
    - `selected_category` (optional, int or None),
    - `location_filter` (optional string)

- `/job/<int:job_id>` [GET]
  - Renders **job-details-page.html**.
  - Context variables:
    - `job` (single job dict),
    - `company` (dict of associated company),
    - `category` (category dict)

- `/companies` [GET]
  - Renders **companies-page.html**.
  - Context variables:
    - `companies` (list of companies)

- `/company/<int:company_id>` [GET]
  - Renders **company-profile-page.html**.
  - Context variables:
    - `company` (dict),
    - `jobs` (list of job dict for company)

- `/applications` [GET]
  - Renders **applications-list.html**.
  - Context variables:
    - `applications` (all applications for user),
    - `jobs` (dict keyed by job_id),
    - `resumes` (dict keyed by resume_id)

- `/application/<int:application_id>` [GET]
  - Renders **application-details-page.html**.
  - Context variables:
    - `application` (dict),
    - `job` (dict),
    - `resume` (dict)

- `/resumes` [GET]
  - Renders **resumes-list.html**.
  - Context variables:
    - `resumes` (list of resumes)

- `/upload_resume` [POST]
  - Handles resume file upload form submission.

- `/apply/<int:job_id>` [POST]
  - Handles job application submission.

- `/delete_resume/<int:resume_id>` [POST]
  - Deletes resume specified.


## 3. Navigation Elements and IDs

The app uses a consistent set of container IDs and button/element IDs in HTML templates to facilitate frontend manipulation and backend referencing.

### Navigation Buttons

- `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Returns to dashboard `/`
- `browse-jobs-button` (Button): Navigate to `/jobs`
- `companies-button` (Button): Navigate to `/companies`
- `my-applications-button` (Button): Navigate to `/applications`
- `upload-resume-button` (Button): Opens resume upload form

### Search and Filters

- `search-input` (Input text): Keyword search for jobs or companies
- `category-filter` (Dropdown select): Filters jobs by category
- `location-filter` (Input text): Filter jobs by location
- `status-filter` (Dropdown select): Filter applications by status

### Listings and Tables

- `jobs-list` (Container Div): Holds grid/list of job cards
- `job-results` (Div): Detailed job search results container
- `companies-list` (Div): List companies
- `applications-table` (Table): Lists all user applications
- `resumes-list` (Table or Div): Lists resumes for user

### Dynamic Buttons (Each render)

- `view-job-button-{job_id}` (Button): View details of a specific job
- `apply-now-button-{job_id}` (Button): Submit application for job
- `view-company-button-{company_id}` (Button): View company profile
- `view-application-button-{application_id}` (Button): View application details
- `delete-resume-button-{resume_id}` (Button): Deletes the given resume


## 4. Template Files and Context Variables

All templates located in the `templates/` directory use Jinja2 syntax. 

- `dashboard.html`
  - Context: `jobs`, `companies`, `applications`, `resumes`
  - Displays widgets summarizing data, with primary navigation buttons.

- `jobs-list.html`
  - Context: `jobs`, `categories`, `selected_category`, `location_filter`
  - Displays search/filter inputs and job postings grid.

- `job-details-page.html`
  - Context: `job`, `company`, `category`
  - Shows detailed job description with apply button.

- `companies-page.html`
  - Context: `companies`
  - Displays company list with navigation buttons.

- `company-profile-page.html`
  - Context: `company`, `jobs`
  - Show company details and current job postings.

- `applications-list.html`
  - Context: `applications`, `jobs`, `resumes`
  - Shows user applications with statuses and links.

- `application-details-page.html`
  - Context: `application`, `job`, `resume`
  - Detailed view of a single application including attached resume info.

- `resumes-list.html`
  - Context: `resumes`
  - Lists user uploaded resumes with delete buttons.

- `application-form-page.html`
  - Context: `job`, `resumes`
  - Form for users to apply for a job, selecting an existing resume or upload a new one.

## 5. Detailed Example of a Route Implementation (Flask style)

```python
@app.route('/job/<int:job_id>', methods=['GET'])
def job_details(job_id):
    job = get_job_by_id(job_id)
    company = get_company_by_id(job['company_id'])
    category = get_category_by_name(job['category'])
    return render_template('job-details-page.html', job=job, company=company, category=category)
```

Use `url_for` in templates leveraging the above route definitions, e.g.: 
```
<a id="view-job-button-{{ job.job_id }}" href="{{ url_for('job_details', job_id=job.job_id) }}">View Job</a>
```

## 6. Summary of IDs and their Types

| ID Pattern | Element Type | Description |
|-------------|--------------|-------------|
| dashboard | Page Container Div | Main dashboard page container |
| back-to-dashboard | Button | Navigation back to main dashboard |
| browse-jobs-button | Button | Navigate to jobs listing |
| companies-button | Button | Navigate to companies listing |
| my-applications-button | Button | Navigate to applications listing |
| jobs-list | Div | Container showing job-card elements |
| view-job-button-{job_id} | Button | View the given job by job_id |
| apply-now-button-{job_id} | Button | Apply for job_id |
| applications-table | Table | Display applications user has submitted |
| view-application-button-{app_id} | Button | View application detail |
| delete-resume-button-{resume_id} | Button | Delete a resume by ID |
